<review>In all my expeditions to numerous wrecking yards in my life in california, one inevitable fact, its a dirty office, someone's takes your 2 dollars and if asked will tell you where auto should be. You scout around all the wrecks that are stacked on rims on gravel with rusty bolts and forms of small parts on the surface. Bring your own tools and there is no T-Mobile service if you need youtube for specific car part removal. So record it if need be with an app first. They provide a 30 day credit or replacement and the wrecker was a very nice and humorous man, son also. Prices are pretty typical. But it is also the second to smallest wrecker I've visited, there is one South of town, that can't have more than 50 vehicles, so if you have a mechanical aptitude they are a good way to save money. <username>Chris Karjanis</username>< review>
This was probably the worst leasing experience I have ever had. I rented a 1 room studio apartment for $2,215 per month (not including utilities and misc. “fees”) for just over 1 year and could never justify the cost. I am relieved to be done with their dealings. The leasing staff even had time to call me to inquire if I had a towel hanging from my balcony, and if so, could I remove it - what kind of place has time for this?! There were other things which occurred during my tenure as well. Please see attached photos in my review of my leasing experience at Westgate Apartments. 1) Garage plumbing leaked profusely next to my vehicle, 2) Mail room was trashed, 3) Neighbor posted to a shared resident site about receiving cruel letter on their door, 4) Water quality was poor (as visible from staining and number of residents ordering water deliveries) which caused functional component of sink to need replacing after leaking all over counter, 5) Multiple bulbs from various fixtures needed replacing, 6) Received a letter about not smoking Marijuana taped to my door from a resident (I do not smoke marijuana, but they should have taped it to the stairwell), 7) My vehicle was burglarized while parked in my designated resident parking spot in the garage; and the remote garage door opener and a bag of change from my (closed) center console were stolen, 8) Water was leaking from the light fixture above my bathtub, 9) I have short hair, but in less than one month from move-in, tub started clogging and I removed a swath of hair over 12 inches long from the bathtub drain, 10) Ice maker had to be replaced, 11) Vehicle parked next to my guests’ in Guest parking was broken into.
As if all this wasn’t enough, they only refunded about $38 of my $600 deposit!  I am so happy to have left this place.</review>

<date>1521043535190< /date><rate>1</rate>< review>
The community looks nice to a potential leasee, but don’t be fooled, it is nice at face value only.  The apartment was not move-in ready, despite having had a set move-in date for nearly 4 months. The unit had not been cleaned, and the cabinets were missing doors and handles. The office staff is rude and slow to respond to resident needs. Maintenance requests often go completely ignored. The electrical work is shoddy and over half of the electrical outlets do not work in our unit. The common areas such as the hallways and outdoor spaces are dirty and have not been cleaned since October (5 months ago). The elevators are 4 months past a required state safety inspection and often jump or stall when residents are in them. The fire alarms go off at all hours of the day, including the middle of the night for 20-40 minutes at a time. The individuals answering the emergency line act as though they have been inconvenienced when called to assist with emergent issues. This community is definitely NOT worth the money.<//review>

I am on my second lease. My first year used to be good. I loved the apartment community, and the leasing team. However, the last few months, the fire alarm went off everyday, in the middle of the night, early in the morning, etc. Now they are fixing the alarm, which is good, but too many office visits because of it. However, this is not my reason for a negative review.

The managment team is very UNPROFESSIONAL. They never take care of things on time. They say it will be done in 2 days, it takes them like at least a week or even few months. Also, I experienced so much negativity when I visit the office to pick up packages, etc. Often I was treated rudely or carelessly for no reason. Hiromi is the only one who actually has a positive attitude in the office.

I lived in so many different Equity Apartments, in north Cal and south Cal for last 7 years. I am experiencing the most unprofessional leasing team in Westgate.

I cannot wait for my lease to end, so I can move out of Westgate. I didn’t have time to move when my first lease ended, and now I regret it so much.

Also, the apartment is not worth the price. Way too expensive for such an old apartment. My second lease, they raised more than 15%! There are better apartment, way newer and cleaner, in the similar price range around the area, SERIOUSLY.

Overall, the apartment is old and was dirty can needed a lot of repair when I moved in. However, I just went along because the leasing team used to be professional and pleasant. However, now the price is unreasonably too high for the quality of the aparment, and the leasing team is unprofessional and unfriendly, which gives me no reason to stay anymore.</review>

<Text>WageWorks is the worst health insurance-related company I have ever encountered, and believe me, after being a client of every major insurer, that is saying something.

I have the misfortune to have WageWorks as my company's COBRA administrator. On July 3, I paid WageWorks electronically to cover insurance for July.  This payment was immediately deducted from my bank account.

WageWorks' job was to submit notification to my insurance company that this payment was made. But today,  on July 12, one of my healthcare providers called to tell they had no record my me having insurance, and my insurance company confirmed this.

Here is how WageWorks' representative explained their process: After you pay, they have FIVE TO SEVEN  business days to "process" your payment. They claim this is a "blackout period," and that they wait until all the payments from everyone are in to process the money.

Then, after they've sat on your money for 5-7 business days, they claim they have ANOTHER 3-5 business days to notify your insurer of your coverage. So today, finally, after me insisting that they act, WageWorks makes an "urgent" notification to my insurance company.

This is not only ridiculous, it is usery.

My former employer was not previously aware of WageWorks' process, but they are now. I hope by making this complaint I can help other people to watch their money when WageWorks is involved.<//Text><pics>None</pics>< response>

< review>
This place and the ladies who work there are wonderful! Lice is not a fun thing to go through and we found that our three kids and us had it. Ugh! We initially bought the kits from CVS since it was late and night and we tried to thoroughly wash and come everything out. The next day my wife found Nit Picky. We made an appt and took the entire family. They were great. Extremely informative, really professional and gentle but extremely thorough with our young kids. They taught us everything we needed to know, showed us how to comb everything out and we ended up purchasing their kit, which was light years better than anything we saw at the store. The lice was gone and with their instructions they didn't come back. They even told us that now that we know everything the next time this happens, if it does in the future, we don't even need to come in we can just do these steps ourselves at home.
That extreme peace of mind that we had when we left was worth it. They also gave all of our kids a signed certificate that they were lice free. Our schools accepted those when we brought them back to school the next day and it excused their absence from the day before.
If you are considering coming here I wouldn't even bother purchasing anything at the store. Come here first and they will help get you on the right path and you will feel totally at ease by the time you leave.</review>

< review>
Pulled in to do a quick vacuum of dirt that got into my car. Got my quarters. Sign said “Tokens Only”, went to Token machine that says “out of service when light is on”, light was NOT on so i put in some quarters, and... NOTHING. Haha. No tokens, took my quarters, and nowhere to find a customer service rep and no sign on how to reach management. I hate to give a bad score because i have such a soft spot in my heart for car washes and memories of going to self serve carwashes with my dad who has since passed. But i feel if you have confidence in your business you would not hide from your customers, you would be open to being reached if any issues. Hope things improve here, thanks.< /review>

< Review>
I am a hobby Yorkshire Terrier breeder. I have brought my dogs here for their shots, and teeth cleaning. The wait can be insanely long sometimes. Even to drop your dog off, with an appointment (teeth cleaning) I had to wait almost 2 hours.
I also had my kitten neutered here. They did a good job, but even though they called me to pick up I still had to wait an hour and a half.
I feel like Dr. Sam was very good. Most of the staff is nice.
But they need to higher a person for just the front desk, to answer phones and take payments. They get really backed up. And it would alleviate stress on the nurses. Plus the nurses wouldn't get so behind.
I took 1 star off because of a couple of the crazy waits.
But I have recommended this hospital to several people, because they make pet care affordable.  And that is a wonderful thing.</Review>

< review>
Back in july i took our frenchie there because he had severe diarrhea and ended up staying there for 5 days. He had no other symptoms so my first thought is salmonella since he did eat cooked chicken before. Turns out he had nothing wrong, no infection nor bacteria ( which made no sense). At pick up i was given antibiotics incase he did have something and that seemed to have been working for him there i guess ( still not making sense). So on my way to the car he coughs and im like "okay" this better not be kennel cough because he didn't have it before". I get home and he's coughing more and i wait a day or two before i call the clinic to make sure it's not a dry throat. They prescribe clavamox and temaril over the phone. So im thinking ok this should work since it just started. I notice neither meds is working but i wait to finish the temaril since it helps open the airways. Let me say i have always worked as a vet tech since i was 17 and stopped about 5-6 yrs ago cuz i had to raise my son. And i know if the meds aren't working its because its beyond just a cough now. I take him back and i tell them i recieved him back sicker, turns out it was a respiratory infection almost turning into broncolitis. Both lungs and heart were inflamed. I was upset because kennel cough is the cause for this and kennel cough is airborne. Meaning the dog who had it wasn't isolated from other dogs or the clinic lacks in sanitizing the exam rooms. I mentioned it to the doc and was given a discount. And to top it off his cough lasted 2 months.
This shouldn't have gone unnoticed, when you are in treatment medicating and observing the pets that stay over night your job is to mention it on the file but it wasn't. This is very irresponsible that means this place isn't being run correctly. Every vet i have ever worked at has one big rule which is " always clean the exam room before and after" and sanitize the floors often and that's something colima does not do. My heart sanked because i know breeders who have gone to colima and had their pups died from a bad respiratory infection.  But we had not experienced it yet up until that day. I understand you techs at colima are busy but a way to make it easier and smoother for everyone is to do what's easy first.
Vaccines, deworming, and progesterone test should be seen first. You don't need to take them to the back or to a room, it can be done in the car or up front. Medication, drop off and pick up can be done by two or 3 girls. And last should be the dogs waiting for an exam. This way things are out of the way and so are people.< /review>

Well no phone call came after 3 p.m. We headed to the vet, something told me something was wrong. Well we went into the office, had to wait another 30 minutes when finally an office assistant said she was ready and she would bring Chata out. She had no knowledge how many pups or if the mom was fine. Well they brought the pups (2) out on a dog bowl like tray (dirty). I asked them, there were only 2 alive? We're there any still born? She responded that there was only 2. I asked to see the doctor immediately, Dr Sam came out and told me that in fact there was only 2, no stillborn. I told him that I had done an ultrasound done on her on her 5th week and that I had proof that there was at least 5 pups. He told me that ultrasound are not accurate, I responded I understand that's why Canine Cryobank said it was definitely 5 or maybe more. I know what I saw and Carrol at Canine Cryobank saw. She was disgusted what happened. Now I have been hearing from the Fenchie community that some breeders have had similar experiences with Colima.BEWARE!! I am waiting for my attorney to open his office, if you have proof or similar experiences like mine contact me PLEASE. No one should be going through this. BTW the Dr told me that videos are recorded for the csection, what are the chances that my girls was not recorded.< /Text>< Date>

I had a very long review drawn up. I guess it never saved.  From what I recall, some of the food wasn't very hot when it was served.  We were sat at a very small seating for 5 after waiting about 20 minutes.  It was hot as hades in there, I don't think they had any AC.  I think the flavor of the food was okay, from what I recall (mostly).  I might try it again, but it sure would be nice if they had some working AC in this place when it's almost 100 degrees outside and the place was crammed. Oh yeah, the sausage was burned and didn't taste that great, and the potatoes were very greasy, I do remember that.  The service was slow.  They also forgot one of our plates initially. Orange juice tasted like it was made from frozen concentrate.

We are new to the area here, but a few people have mentioned that this is the best breakfast place in town and not to bother going anywhere else.  That makes me wonder if that is the case. If so, that's sad.  For the price, I felt the food was just "meh".< /text>

<Date>1550821174810< /Date><rating>1< /rating><Review>This location is not a reflection of the other Waffle Shops I have been to and enjoyed, and maybe they were just having a bad morning at this location. This was my first time to this location so it's all I have to rate it on........ From where my table was I could see into the kitchen and proceeded to watch one of the cooks only wearing one glove while working, while the other cooks had on two. This cook while wearing the same glove wiped counters, handled the broom stick and swept. Then proceeded to use that glove hand to handle plates and utensils while using his bare hand to take the waffles off the grill and put them on the plates. I watched all this for at least 20mins, and he never changed the glove or washed his hand(s) between activities. And while all this was happening another staff memeber was constantly yelling loudly at the busboy to clean tables faster, even though he was the only one doing tables for the whole place during a busy morning. And then when my food finally came my gf's omelette was cool to the touch and the cheese wasn't melted. They poured strawberries out of a jar onto my waffle, that had already been handled with a bare hand, causing it to be the consistency of bread sitting in water. So needless to say we did not eat our food and left. I try very hard to not leave bad reviews because I believe a business is trying their best and bad reviews can hurt a families well being, but what I saw that morning was ridiculous.</Review>< pictures>

< review>
I have 3 stars because I think it could have been better all around. My son had a dentist appointment across the lot so aftwards we stopped in for breakfast. I looked the shop up on Google before we went. Just to read some reviews, menu prices and such. The prices were good, not too expensive. Once we grabbed a seat and got our menus,  the prices were off, by a couple dollars,  online it read prices around $5-6 a plate, the actual prices were around $8-9!. The waitress was very cold with her greeting and mannerisms. She only came by once to see if everything was ok. And they didn't have a lot of what we were wanting to order. My son wanted a strawberry waffle with vanilla ice cream and a chocolate milk. But they didn't have any ice cream nor chocolate milk.  He ended up with a regular waffle with strawberries and whip cream with a hot chocolate (mind you, here in central California it's 105° today).  I ordered the waffle combo. (1 waffle, 2 eggs and 3 sausage links) and an iced tea. I ordered the eggs scrambled, they came to the table cold with the sausage that looked burnt. My bill came to $49.81! The only time the waitress was polite was when I was paying the bill. I don't think we will be going back there. It really was not worth $49 for my 14 year old and myself. Especially since we couldn't get what we really wanted to eat. Needless to say,  I did not leave a tip.<//review>
